This is a very clever song alongside Eminem's song Stan, it's a stalker song. The video shows a young sweet looking girl getting ready for a night out with her mates, in contrast  CC is portrayed as a lonely figure in a bedsit in a run down sea side town and there are plenty of those areas in the UK. The girl in question is getting on with her night having fun with her mates whilst said , "without sounding too perverted", solitary guy, is in his room fantasizing about her body grooming, making assumptions about her hopes and desires for the future etc, that she wants rough sex, even who bought her bracelet!, yet he doesn't even know her.  I remember going out wearing a shirt and high heels and nothing else when I was a young girl, not to get male attention but just to show how fashionable and cool I was. We all go out looking for fun but the girl comes home content to a degree, after her kebab, while the guy in the bedsit seems sinister and has an agenda. Well observed CC, it shows the mismatched dialogue and hopes that often are perpetuated by young guys living in some sort of wasteland of macho delusions who are probably just as lonely and in need of affection as the rest of us.
